 Since 2013, 16 countries including India have been involved in negotiations on a major trade deal
 inamen dakshin purv asian deshon ke sanghathan (asian) ke 10 sadsy or iske chah mukt-vyapaar bhagidaar—bharat, china, dakshin korea, japan, australiya or newjiland—shaamil he
 Called the Regional Comprehensive Economic Partnership (RCEP), the deal could become the largest economic bloc, accounting for 39 percent of the world's total GDP
 is baatcheet kii samay-seemaa 4 november he, jab iske sabhi raashtra pramukh aarasieepi leaders shikhar sammelan ke liye baithak karenge

 prastaavit aarasieepi saude ke vaartakar 10 aktubar tak iske 25 khandon main se 21 par raji ho chuke the
 The remaining four sections — those related to investment, e-commerce, rules of origin and the redress of business — have not yet been agreed
 isamen tarriff ek badi baadha bani hui he kyonki bharat kii maang he ki samvedansheel vastuon kii zyada badi sankhya ko 'auto-trigar mekensm' (jisamen aayaat shulk ek seemaa ke baad swat: bad jaataa he) ke yogya rakhaa janaa chahie
 India is also seeking to make 2019 a base year for enumeration and to remove different tariff rates with RCEP members
 aarasieepi ke zyaadaatar sadasyon kaa kahana he ki shulk ek baar kam ho jane ke baad unhen dobaaraa nahin badhaayaa janaa chahie

 needed
 bharat kii chintaa apane gharelu udyog ko lekar he
